			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, increased 28 percent in the first quarter when compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. This increase is </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">driven by increased demand linked to renovation trends associated with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">pandemic and increased sales through the ecommerce channel</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">15 percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the first quarter compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">year fiscal quarter.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We experienced a significant increase in sales of our homecare and cleaning products </font>

The quarterly dividend is </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">payable </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">on January </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">29</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">to stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">January </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.</font>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On April 8, 2020, the Company elected to suspend repurchases under its previously approved share buy-back plan, which subsequently expired on August 31, 2020. The Company made this election in order to preserve cash while it continues to monitor the long-term impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic. Management does not expect to seek Board approval for a new share buy-back plan until it starts to see a reduced level of uncertainty regarding the pandemic&#x2019;s impact on the economy and the Company&#x2019;s business. Therefore, no repurchase transactions were made during the first quarter of fiscal year 2021</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a wide range of maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;, Lava&#xAE; and Solvol&#xAE;.&nbsp; </font>

WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
